    Introduction

    This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

    As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

    Base URL

    http://fulcrum.test

    Authenticating requests

    This API is not authenticated.

    BidAmount management

    APIs for managing Bid Amount

    Display a listing of the resource.

    Example request:
    curl --request GET \
    --get "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
    const url = new URL(
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

    Request      

    GET api/amount

    Store a newly created resource in storage.

    Example request:
    curl --request POST \
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"price\": \"100\",
    \"status\": 0,
    \"bid_id\": 1
}"

    const url = new URL(
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "price": "100",
    "status": 0,
    "bid_id": 1
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
    Received response:
    Request failed with error:

    Request      

    POST api/amount

    Body Parameters

    price  string  

    The amount of the bid.

    status  integer optional  

    The status of the bid.

    bid_id  integer optional  

    the id of the bid.

    Display the specified resource.

    Example request:
    curl --request GET \
    --get "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount/15" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
    const url = new URL(
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount/15"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

    Example response (200):

    Show headers 
    cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
access-control-allow-origin: *

    Request      

    GET api/amount/{id}

    URL Parameters

    id  integer  

    The ID of the amount.

    Update the specified resource in storage.

    Example request:
    curl --request PUT \
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount/4" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"price\": \"100\",
    \"status\": 0,
    \"bid_id\": 1
}"

    const url = new URL(
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount/4"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "price": "100",
    "status": 0,
    "bid_id": 1
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
    Received response:
    Request failed with error:

    Request      

    PUT api/amount/{id}

    PATCH api/amount/{id}

    URL Parameters

    id  integer  

    The ID of the amount.

    Body Parameters

    price  string  

    The amount of the bid.

    status  integer optional  

    The status of the bid.

    bid_id  integer optional  

    the id of the bid.

    Remove the specified resource from storage.

    Example request:
    curl --request DELETE \
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount/15" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
    const url = new URL(
    "http://fulcrum.test/api/amount/15"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
    Received response:
    Request failed with error:

    Request      

    DELETE api/amount/{id}

    URL Parameters

    id  integer  

    The ID of the amount.
